<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On August 26, 2004, Cascade Corporation issued a press
release announcing results for its second fiscal quarter ended July 31, 2004,
and held a conference call regarding the results.&#160; The press release is included as Exhibit 99.1
and the transcript is included as Exhibit 99.2 to this Form 8-K.&#160; This discussion, as well as the press release
and the transcript, shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18 of
the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 or incorporated by reference in any filing
under the Securities Act of 1933.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h4 style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-decoration:underline;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></u></b></h4>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CASCADE
CORPORATION ANNOUNCES EARNINGS OF $0.51 PER SHARE FOR THE QUARTER ENDED JULY
31, 2004</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Cascade
Corporation (NYSE: CAE) today reported its financial results for the second
quarter ended July 31, 2004.</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Second Quarter Fiscal 2005 Summary</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Summary financial results for the second
quarter and results for the comparable quarter of the previous year are
outlined below (in thousands, except earnings per share):</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cascade Corporation</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">August 26, 2004</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Consolidated gross profit percentage
decreased to 32% as compared to 33% in the comparable quarter of the prior
year.&#160; This decrease was due primarily to
higher materials costs.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The majority of the increase in SG&amp;A was
attributable to implementation of Sarbanes-Oxley requirements, increased
R&amp;D expenses and SG&amp;A attributable to Roncari Srl, acquired during the
third quarter of fiscal 2004.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The increase in amortization expense was
primarily due to compensation expense related to stock appreciation rights.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The increase in the effective tax rate from
32% to 36% was due primarily to decreased benefits from international financing
activities and an increase in valuation allowances on deferred tax assets in
Europe.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Market Conditions</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">FY05 second quarter shipments in the North
American lift truck market were up 14% over the second quarter of FY04 and up
10% for the first six months of FY 05 as compared to the same period in
FY04.&#160; Shipments and orders are now in
approximate equilibrium.&#160; With the
current industry backlog, lift truck shipments should remain strong at least
through the next quarter.&#160;&#160; Although&#160; lift truck shipments are an indicator of the
general health of the industry, they do not necessarily correlate with the
demand for Cascade&#146;s products.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">FY05 second quarter shipments in the European
lift truck market were up 22% over the second quarter of FY04 and up 13% for
the first six months of FY05 as compared to the first six months of FY04.&#160; Orders were up 18% year-to-date over the prior
year. We are cautiously optimistic about the European lift truck market for the
balance of the year.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">FY05 second quarter shipments in the
Asia-Pacific lift truck market were up 22% as compared to the second quarter of
FY04 and up 23% for the first six months of FY05 as compared to the same period
in FY04.&#160; For the first six months of
FY05 order rates were up 26% over the prior year.&#160; We continue to see strength in the
Asia-Pacific region as a whole&#160; and in
the Chinese market in particular.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Steel costs have increased more rapidly than
expected for many of the steel grades used in our products.&#160; We are aggressively working to mitigate these
increases through a variety of means.&#160;&#160;
We will continue these efforts in the coming months, although there is
no assurance we will be able to mitigate the full impact of all steel cost
increases.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">2</font></b></p>

<div style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></b></div>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Revenue growth reflected the strong North
American lift truck market in the second quarter, which resulted in increased
second quarter shipments.&#160; Revenues were
also favorably impacted by the current US$/Euro exchange rate, which&#160; has served to reduce European imports into
the North American market.&#160;&#160;&#160; Details of
the revenue increase for the quarter over the prior year quarter follow (in
thousands):</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.25in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The increase in gross profit percentage was a
result of higher volumes in all North American factories resulting in better
fixed cost absorption.&#160; North America has
not yet experienced steel price increases as dramatic as those&#160; in Europe and we believe early pricing
adjustments have largely covered our materials cost increases to date.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Increased SG&amp;A expense was primarily attributable
to implementation of Sarbanes-Oxley requirements and increased R&amp;D expense.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The increase in amortization expense was
primarily due to compensation expense related to stock appreciation rights.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Gross margins declined primarily due to
higher steel costs and increased sales of lower margin OEM products.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

effects of both foreign exchange and&#160;
additional SG&amp;A attributable to Roncari Srl, an acquisition made in
the third quarter of FY04.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">The increase in SG&amp;A was due to the
effect of strengthening foreign currencies and continued&#160; expansion of our sales and service support
capabilities in the Chinese market.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Dividend</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#149;</font></b><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">On August 24, 2004, the Company&#146;s Board of
Directors declared a quarterly dividend of $.11 per share, payable on October
7, 2004 to shareholders of record as of September 22, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">President &amp; CEO Comments</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Robert C.
Warren, Jr., President and Chief Executive Officer, remarked&#160; &#147;We are pleased with our results in the
second quarter, particularly in light of rapidly increasing steel prices which
were greater than expected, particularly in Europe. &#160;Although we believe we have been able to
mitigate these increases in most cases, timing price increases to coincide with
actual cost increases has been, and will continue to be somewhat difficult.&#148;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Mr.
Warren further commented that &#147;We remain cautiously optimistic about the next
quarter due to the substantial backlog in the North American lift truck market
and the continuing strength in Asia.&#160;
However, our outlook beyond the third quarter is uncertain.&#160; A measurable economic slowdown in any of our
major world markets would undoubtedly have an adverse impact on our
business.&#160; Our results in Europe also
continue to reflect the highly competitive environment in our industry and we
do not foresee any significant change in this situation in the near
future.&#160; I would like to note that we are
continuing to negotiate the purchase of Falkenroth Foerdertechnik, a
significant&#160; European competitor
currently in&#160; receivership.&#148;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></b></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release
contains forward-looking statements made pursuant to the Safe Harbor provisions
of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.&#160; Readers are cautioned that a number of
factors could cause our actual results to differ materially from any results
indicated in this release or in any other forward-looking statements made by
us, or on our behalf.&#160; These include
among others factors related to general economic conditions, interest rates,
demand for materials handling products, performance of our manufacturing
facilities and the cyclical nature of the materials handling industry.&#160; Further, historical information should not be
considered an indicator of future performance. Additional considerations and
important risk factors are described in our reports on Form 10-K and 10-Q and
other filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Cascade Corporation:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cascade Corporation, headquartered in Fairview, Oregon, is a leading
international manufacturer of materials handling products used primarily on
lift trucks.&#160; Additional information on
Cascade is available on its website, www.cascorp.com.</font></p>

  prices have been up 50%. We&#146;ve seen really significant increases but probably
  more in the 30-40% across the range. There&#146;s about 3 moving parts in that
  gross margin in Europe, Frank. The steel is most definitely a very
  significant portion of it and we experienced the increase. We put in during
  the quarter our price increases but those increases were for future
  shipments, the shipments we were making on the higher steel. We had a little
  timing, maybe more than a little timing issue on some of those and that
  continues to be something as the volatility of the market continues that our
  ability to match exactly the invoices of shipments with the increase of
  incoming steel is not perfect.</font></p>
